[End Tag        ] </a>

[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Comparison_of_layout_engines_(HTML5_canvas)' title='Comparison of layout engines (HTML5 canvas)'>
[Text           ] canvas
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </li>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Comparison_of_layout_engines_(HTML5_media)' title='Comparison of layout engines (HTML5 media)'>
[Text           ] media
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] )
[End Tag        ] </li>
[End Tag        ] </ul>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </li>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Comparison_of_layout_engines_(XHTML)' title='Comparison of layout engines (XHTML)'>
[Text           ] XHTML
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] &nbsp;(
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Comparison_of_layout_engines_(XHTML_1.1)' title='Comparison of layout engines (XHTML 1.1)'>
[Text           ] 1.1
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] )
[End Tag        ] </li>
[End Tag        ] </ul>
[End Tag        ] </td>
[End Tag        ] </tr>

[End Tag        ] </table>

[End Tag        ] </tr>

[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Start Tag      ] <b>
[Text           ] HyperText Markup Language
[End Tag        ] </b>
[Text           ] , commonly referred to as
[Start Tag      ] <b>
[Text           ] HTML
[End Tag        ] </b>
[Text           ] , is the standard
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Markup_language' title='Markup language'>
[Text           ] markup language
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] used to create
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Web_page' title='Web page'>
[Text           ] web pages
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] .
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-1' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-1'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 1
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] It is written in the form of
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML_element' title='HTML element'>
[Text           ] HTML elements
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] consisting of
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] tags
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] enclosed in
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bracket#Angle_brackets' title='Bracket'>
[Text           ] angle brackets
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] (like
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;html&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] ). HTML tags most commonly come in pairs like
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;h1&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] and
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;/h1&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] , although some tags represent
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] empty elements
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] and so are unpaired, for example
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;img&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] . The first tag in a pair is the
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] start tag
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] , and the second tag is the
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] end tag
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] (they are also called
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] opening tags
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] and
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] closing tags
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] ).
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Web_browser' title='Web browser'>
[Text           ] Web browsers
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] can read HTML files and compose them into visible or audible web pages. Browsers do not display the HTML tags and scripts, but use them to interpret the content of the page. HTML describes the structure of a
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Website' title='Website'>
[Text           ] website
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semantic' title='Semantic' class='mw-redirect'>
[Text           ] semantically
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] along with cues for presentation, making it a markup language, rather than a
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language' title='Programming language'>
[Text           ] programming language
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] .
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] HTML elements form the building blocks of all websites. HTML allows
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Img_(HTML_element)' title='Img (HTML element)' class='mw-redirect'>
[Text           ] images and objects
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] to be embedded and can be used to create
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fieldset' title='Fieldset' class='mw-redirect'>
[Text           ] interactive forms
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] . It provides a means to create
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Structured_document' title='Structured document'>
[Text           ] structured documents
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] by denoting structural semantics for text such as headings, paragraphs, lists,
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hyperlink' title='Hyperlink'>
[Text           ] links
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] , quotes and other items. It can embed
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scripting_language' title='Scripting language'>
[Text           ] scripts
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] written in languages such as
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/JavaScript' title='JavaScript'>
[Text           ] JavaScript
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] which affect the behavior of HTML web pages.
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] Web browsers can also refer to
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cascading_Style_Sheets' title='Cascading Style Sheets'>
[Text           ] Cascading Style Sheets
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] (CSS) to define the look and layout of text and other material. The
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/World_Wide_Web_Consortium' title='World Wide Web Consortium'>
[Text           ] World Wide Web Consortium
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] (W3C), maintainer of both the HTML and the CSS standards, encourages the use of CSS over explicit presentational HTML.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-deprecated_2-0' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-deprecated-2'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 2
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <div id='toc' class='toc'>

[Text           ] An example website written in HTML Code
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[Start Tag      ] <h3>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-headline' id='Development'>
[Text           ] Development
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection'>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection-bracket'>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=HTML&action=edit&section=2' title='Edit section: Development'>
[Text           ] edit
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection-bracket'>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </h3>
[Start Tag      ] <div class='thumb tright'>
[Start Tag      ] <div class='thumbinner' style='width:172px;'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Tim_Berners-Lee_April_2009.jpg' class='image'>
[Start Tag      ] <img alt src='./wikipedia_files/170px-Tim_Berners-Lee_April_2009.jpg' width='170' height='234' class='thumbimage' srcset='//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Tim_Berners-Lee_April_2009.jpg/255px-Tim_Berners-Lee_April_2009.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Tim_Berners-Lee_April_2009.jpg/340px-Tim_Berners-Lee_April_2009.jpg 2x' data-file-width='1195' data-file-height='1648'>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Start Tag      ] <div class='thumbcaption'>
[Start Tag      ] <div class='magnify'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Tim_Berners-Lee_April_2009.jpg' class='internal' title='Enlarge'>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tim_Berners-Lee' title='Tim Berners-Lee'>
[Text           ] Tim Berners-Lee
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] In 1980, physicist
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tim_Berners-Lee' title='Tim Berners-Lee'>
[Text           ] Tim Berners-Lee
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] , who was a contractor at
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/CERN' title='CERN'>
[Text           ] CERN
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] , proposed and prototyped
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ENQUIRE' title='ENQUIRE'>
[Text           ] ENQUIRE
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] , a system for CERN researchers to use and share documents. In 1989, Berners-Lee wrote a memo proposing an
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet' title='Internet'>
[Text           ] Internet
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] -based
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hypertext' title='Hypertext'>
[Text           ] hypertext
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] system.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-3' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-3'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 3
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] Berners-Lee specified HTML and wrote the browser and server software in late 1990. That year, Berners-Lee and CERN data systems engineer
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Cailliau' title='Robert Cailliau'>
[Text           ] Robert Cailliau
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] collaborated on a joint request for funding, but the project was not formally adopted by CERN. In his personal notes
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-4' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-4'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 4
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] from 1990 he listed
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-5' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-5'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 5
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] "some of the many areas in which hypertext is used" and put an encyclopedia first.
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] The first publicly available description of HTML was a document called "HTML Tags", first mentioned on the Internet by Berners-Lee in late 1991.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-tagshtml_6-0' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-tagshtml-6'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 6
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-7' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-7'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 7
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] It describes 18 elements comprising the initial, relatively simple design of HTML. Except for the hyperlink tag, these were strongly influenced by
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SGMLguid' title='SGMLguid'>
[Text           ] SGMLguid
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] , an in-house
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_Generalized_Markup_Language' title='Standard Generalized Markup Language'>
[Text           ] Standard Generalized Markup Language
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] (SGML)-based documentation format at CERN. Eleven of these elements still exist in HTML 4.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-8' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-8'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 8
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] HTML is a
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Markup_language' title='Markup language'>
[Text           ] markup language
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] that
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Web_browser' title='Web browser'>
[Text           ] web browsers
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] use to interpret and
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Typesetting' title='Typesetting'>
[Text           ] compose
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] text, images and other material into visual or audible web pages. Default characteristics for every item of HTML markup are defined in the browser, and these characteristics can be altered or enhanced by the web page designer's additional use of
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cascading_Style_Sheets' title='Cascading Style Sheets'>
[Text           ] CSS
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] . Many of the text elements are found in the 1988 ISO technical report TR 9537
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] Techniques for using SGML
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] , which in turn covers the features of early text formatting languages such as that used by the
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/TYPSET_and_RUNOFF' title='TYPSET and RUNOFF'>
[Text           ] RUNOFF command
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] developed in the early 1960s for the
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Compatible_Time-Sharing_System' title='Compatible Time-Sharing System'>
[Text           ] CTSS
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] (Compatible Time-Sharing System) operating system: these formatting commands were derived from the commands used by typesetters to manually format documents. However, the SGML concept of generalized markup is based on elements (nested annotated ranges with attributes) rather than merely print effects, with also the separation of structure and markup; HTML has been progressively moved in this direction with CSS.
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] Berners-Lee considered HTML to be an application of SGML. It was formally defined as such by the
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet_Engineering_Task_Force' title='Internet Engineering Task Force'>
[Text           ] Internet Engineering Task Force
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] (IETF) with the mid-1993 publication of the first proposal for an HTML specification:
[Start Tag      ] <a rel='nofollow' class='external text' href='http://www.w3.org/MarkUp/draft-ietf-iiir-html-01.txt'>
[Text           ] "Hypertext Markup Language (HTML)" Internet-Draft
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] by Berners-Lee and
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dan_Connolly_(computer_scientist)' title='Dan Connolly (computer scientist)'>
[Text           ] Dan Connolly
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] , which included an SGML
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Document_Type_Definition' title='Document Type Definition' class='mw-redirect'>
[Text           ] Document Type Definition
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] to define the grammar.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-9' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-9'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 9
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] The draft expired after six months, but was notable for its acknowledgment of the
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mosaic_(web_browser)' title='Mosaic (web browser)'>
[Text           ] NCSA Mosaic
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] browser's custom tag for embedding in-line images, reflecting the IETF's philosophy of basing standards on successful prototypes.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-raymond_10-0' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-raymond-10'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 10
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] Similarly,
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dave_Raggett' title='Dave Raggett'>
[Text           ] Dave Raggett
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] 's competing Internet-Draft, "HTML+ (Hypertext Markup Format)", from late 1993, suggested standardizing already-implemented features like tables and fill-out forms.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-html.2B_11-0' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-html.2B-11'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 11
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] After the HTML and HTML+ drafts expired in early 1994, the IETF created an HTML Working Group, which in 1995 completed "HTML 2.0", the first HTML specification intended to be treated as a standard against which future implementations should be based.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-12' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-12'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 12
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] Further development under the auspices of the IETF was stalled by competing interests. Since 1996, the HTML specifications have been maintained, with input from commercial software vendors, by the
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/World_Wide_Web_Consortium' title='World Wide Web Consortium'>
[Text           ] World Wide Web Consortium
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] (W3C).
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-raggett_13-0' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-raggett-13'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 13
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] However, in 2000, HTML also became an international standard (
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Organization_for_Standardization' title='International Organization for Standardization'>
[Text           ] ISO
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] /
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Electrotechnical_Commission' title='International Electrotechnical Commission'>
[Text           ] IEC
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] 15445:2000). HTML 4.01 was published in late 1999, with further errata published through 2001. In 2004 development began on HTML5 in the
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Web_Hypertext_Application_Technology_Working_Group' title='Web Hypertext Application Technology Working Group' class='mw-redirect'>
[Text           ] Web Hypertext Application Technology Working Group
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] (WHATWG), which became a joint deliverable with the W3C in 2008, and completed and standardized on 28 October 2014.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-14' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-14'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 14
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <h3>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-headline' id='HTML_versions_timeline'>
[Text           ] HTML versions timeline
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection'>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection-bracket'>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=HTML&action=edit&section=3' title='Edit section: HTML versions timeline'>
[Text           ] edit
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection-bracket'>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </h3>

[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Ambox_current_red.svg' class='image'>
[Start Tag      ] <img alt='Ambox current red.svg' src='./wikipedia_files/42px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png' width='42' height='34' srcset='//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/63px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/84px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 2x' data-file-width='360' data-file-height='290'>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </td>
[Start Tag      ] <td class='mbox-text'>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mbox-text-span'>
[Text           ] Parts of this article (those related to HTML5) are
[Start Tag      ] <b>
[Text           ] outdated
[End Tag        ] </b>
[Text           ] .
[Start Tag      ] <span class='hide-when-compact'>
[Text           ] Please update this article to reflect recent events or newly available information.
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <small>
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] (October 2014)
[End Tag        ] </i>
[End Tag        ] </small>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </td>
[End Tag        ] </tr>
[End Tag        ] </tbody>
[End Tag        ] </table>
[Start Tag      ] <dl>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] November 24, 1995
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] HTML 2.0 was published as IETF
[Start Tag      ] <a class='external mw-magiclink-rfc' rel='nofollow' href='http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc1866'>
[Text           ] RFC 1866
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] . Supplemental
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Request_for_Comments' title='Request for Comments'>
[Text           ] RFCs
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] added capabilities:
[Start Tag      ] <ul>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] November 25, 1995:
[Start Tag      ] <a class='external mw-magiclink-rfc' rel='nofollow' href='http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc1867'>
[Text           ] RFC 1867
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] (form-based file upload)
[End Tag        ] </li>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] May 1996:
[Start Tag      ] <a class='external mw-magiclink-rfc' rel='nofollow' href='http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc1942'>
[Text           ] RFC 1942
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] (tables)
[End Tag        ] </li>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] August 1996:
[Start Tag      ] <a class='external mw-magiclink-rfc' rel='nofollow' href='http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc1980'>
[Text           ] RFC 1980
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] (client-side image maps)
[End Tag        ] </li>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] January 1997:
[Start Tag      ] <a class='external mw-magiclink-rfc' rel='nofollow' href='http://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc2070'>
[Text           ] RFC 2070
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] (
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internationalization_and_localization' title='Internationalization and localization'>
[Text           ] internationalization
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] )
[End Tag        ] </li>
[End Tag        ] </ul>
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[End Tag        ] </dl>
[Start Tag      ] <dl>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] January 1997
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] HTML 3.2
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-15' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-15'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 15
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] was published as a
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/W3C_Recommendation' title='W3C Recommendation' class='mw-redirect'>
[Text           ] W3C Recommendation
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] . It was the first version developed and standardized exclusively by the W3C, as the IETF had closed its HTML Working Group in September 1996.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-16' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-16'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 16
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] Initially code-named "Wilbur",
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-engelfriet_17-0' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-engelfriet-17'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 17
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] HTML 3.2 dropped math formulas entirely, reconciled overlap among various proprietary extensions and adopted most of
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netscape' title='Netscape'>
[Text           ] Netscape
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] 's visual markup tags. Netscape's
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blink_element' title='Blink element'>
[Text           ] blink element
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] and
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microsoft' title='Microsoft'>
[Text           ] Microsoft
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] 's
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marquee_element' title='Marquee element'>
[Text           ] marquee element
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] were omitted due to a mutual agreement between the two companies.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-raggett_13-1' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-raggett-13'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 13
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] A markup for mathematical formulas similar to that in HTML was not standardized until 14 months later in
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/MathML' title='MathML'>
[Text           ] MathML
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] .
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] December 1997
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] HTML 4.0
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-18' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-18'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 18
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] was published as a W3C Recommendation . It offers three variations:
[Start Tag      ] <ul>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] Strict, in which deprecated elements are forbidden,
[End Tag        ] </li>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] Transitional, in which deprecated elements are allowed,
[End Tag        ] </li>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] Frameset, in which mostly only
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Framing_(World_Wide_Web)' title='Framing (World Wide Web)'>
[Text           ] frame
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] related elements are allowed.
[End Tag        ] </li>
[End Tag        ] </ul>
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] Initially code-named "Cougar",
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-engelfriet_17-1' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-engelfriet-17'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 17
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] HTML 4.0 adopted many browser-specific element types and attributes, but at the same time sought to phase out Netscape's visual markup features by marking them as
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Deprecation' title='Deprecation'>
[Text           ] deprecated
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] in favor of style sheets. HTML 4 is an SGML application conforming to ISO 8879&nbsp; SGML.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-19' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-19'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 19
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] April 1998
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] HTML 4.0
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-20' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-20'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 20
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] was reissued with minor edits without incrementing the version number.
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] December 1999
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] HTML 4.01
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-21' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-21'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 21
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] was published as a W3C Recommendation. It offers the same three variations as HTML 4.0 and its last
[Start Tag      ] <a rel='nofollow' class='external text' href='http://www.w3.org/MarkUp/html4-updates/errata'>
[Text           ] errata
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] were published May 12, 2001.
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] May 2000
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] ISO/IEC 15445:2000
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-iso-html_22-0' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-iso-html-22'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 22
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-23' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-23'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 23
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] ("
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Organization_for_Standardization' title='International Organization for Standardization'>
[Text           ] ISO
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] HTML", based on HTML 4.01 Strict) was published as an ISO/IEC international standard. In the ISO this standard falls in the domain of the
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO/IEC_JTC1/SC34' title='ISO/IEC JTC1/SC34' class='mw-redirect'>
[Text           ] ISO/IEC JTC1/SC34
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] (ISO/IEC Joint Technical Committee 1, Subcommittee 34&nbsp; Document description and processing languages).
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-iso-html_22-1' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-iso-html-22'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 22
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] As of mid-2008, HTML 4.01 and ISO/IEC 15445:2000 were the most recent versions of HTML. Development of the parallel, XML-based language XHTML occupied the W3C's HTML Working Group through the early and mid-2000s.
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] October 2014
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] HTML5
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-24' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-24'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 24
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] was published as a W3C Recommendation.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-25' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-25'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 25
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[End Tag        ] </dl>
[Start Tag      ] <h4>

[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] October 1991
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] HTML Tags
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] ,
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-tagshtml_6-1' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-tagshtml-6'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 6
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] an informal CERN document listing 18 HTML tags, was first mentioned in public.
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] June 1992
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] First informal draft of the HTML DTD,
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-26' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-26'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 26
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] with seven
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-27' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-27'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 27
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-28' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-28'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 28
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-html11_29-0' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-html11-29'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 29
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] subsequent revisions (July 15, August 6, August 18, November 17, November 19, November 20, November 22)
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] November 1992
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] HTML DTD 1.1 (the first with a version number, based on RCS revisions, which start with 1.1 rather than 1.0), an informal draft
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-html11_29-1' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-html11-29'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 29
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] June 1993
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] Hypertext Markup Language
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-30' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-30'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 30
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] was published by the
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet_Engineering_Task_Force' title='Internet Engineering Task Force'>
[Text           ] IETF
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] IIIR Working Group as an Internet-Draft (a rough proposal for a standard). It was replaced by a second version
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-ietfiiir_31-0' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-ietfiiir-31'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 31
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] one month later, followed by six further drafts published by IETF itself
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-32' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-32'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 32
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] that finally led to HTML 2.0 in RFC1866
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] November 1993
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] HTML+ was published by the IETF as an Internet-Draft and was a competing proposal to the Hypertext Markup Language draft. It expired in May 1994.
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] April 1995 (authored March 1995)
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] HTML 3.0
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-33' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-33'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 33
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] was proposed as a standard to the IETF, but the proposal expired five months later (28 September 1995)
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-html30cover_34-0' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-html30cover-34'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 34
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] without further action. It included many of the capabilities that were in Raggett's HTML+ proposal, such as support for tables, text flow around figures and the display of complex mathematical formulas.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-html30cover_34-1' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-html30cover-34'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 34
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] W3C began development of its own
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arena_(web_browser)' title='Arena (web browser)'>
[Text           ] Arena browser
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] as a
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Test_bed' title='Test bed' class='mw-redirect'>
[Text           ] test bed
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] for HTML 3 and Cascading Style Sheets,
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-35' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-35'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 35
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-36' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-36'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 36
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-37' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-37'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 37
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] but HTML 3.0 did not succeed for several reasons. The draft was considered very large at 150 pages and the pace of browser development, as well as the number of interested parties, had outstripped the resources of the IETF.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-raggett_13-2' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-raggett-13'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 13
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] Browser vendors, including Microsoft and Netscape at the time, chose to implement different subsets of HTML 3's draft features as well as to introduce their own extensions to it.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-raggett_13-3' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-raggett-13'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 13
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] (See
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Browser_wars' title='Browser wars'>
[Text           ] Browser wars
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] ) These included extensions to control stylistic aspects of documents, contrary to the "belief [of the academic engineering community] that such things as text color, background texture, font size and font face were definitely outside the scope of a language when their only intent was to specify how a document would be organized."
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-raggett_13-4' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-raggett-13'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 13
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] Dave Raggett, who has been a W3C Fellow for many years has commented for example, "To a certain extent, Microsoft built its business on the Web by extending HTML features."
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-raggett_13-5' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-raggett-13'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 13
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] January 2008
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML5' title='HTML5'>
[Text           ] HTML5
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] was published as a
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/World_Wide_Web_Consortium#Recommendations_and_Certifications' title='World Wide Web Consortium'>
[Text           ] Working Draft
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] (
[Start Tag      ] <a rel='nofollow' class='external text' href='http://www.w3.org/TR/html5/'>
[Text           ] link
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] ) by the W3C.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-38' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-38'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 38
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] Although its syntax closely resembles that of
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SGML' title='SGML' class='mw-redirect'>
[Text           ] SGML
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] ,
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML5' title='HTML5'>
[Text           ] HTML5
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] has abandoned any attempt to be an SGML application and has explicitly defined its own "html" serialization, in addition to an alternative XML-based XHTML5 serialization.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-39' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-39'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 39
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] May 2011
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] On 14 February 2011, the W3C extended the charter of its
[Start Tag      ] <a rel='nofollow' class='external text' href='http://www.w3.org/html/wg/'>
[Text           ] HTML Working Group
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] with clear milestones for HTML5. In May 2011, the working group advanced HTML5 to "Last Call", an invitation to communities inside and outside W3C to confirm the technical soundness of the specification. The W3C is developing a comprehensive test suite to achieve broad interoperability for the full specification by 2014, which is now the target date for Recommendation.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-w3c2014_40-0' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-w3c2014-40'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 40
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </dd>
[End Tag        ] </dl>
[Start Tag      ] <h4>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-headline' id='XHTML_versions'>
[Text           ] XHTML versions
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection'>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection-bracket'>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=HTML&action=edit&section=5' title='Edit section: XHTML versions'>
[Text           ] edit
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection-bracket'>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </h4>
[Start Tag      ] <div class='hatnote relarticle mainarticle'>
[Text           ] Main article:
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/XHTML' title='XHTML'>
[Text           ] XHTML
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] XHTML is a separate language that began as a reformulation of HTML 4.01 using
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/XML' title='XML'>
[Text           ] XML
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] 1.0. It is no longer being developed as a separate standard.
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <ul>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] XHTML 1.0,
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-41' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-41'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 41
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] published January 26, 2000, as a W3C Recommendation, later revised and republished August 1, 2002. It offers the same three variations as HTML 4.0 and 4.01, reformulated in XML, with minor restrictions.
[End Tag        ] </li>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] XHTML 1.1,
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-42' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-42'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 42
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] published May 31, 2001, as a W3C Recommendation. It is based on XHTML 1.0 Strict, but includes minor changes, can be customized, is reformulated using modules from
[Start Tag      ] <a rel='nofollow' class='external text' href='http://www.w3.org/TR/xhtml-modularization/'>
[Text           ] Modularization of XHTML
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] , which was published April 10, 2001, as a W3C Recommendation.
[End Tag        ] </li>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] XHTML 2.0 was a working draft, but work on it was abandoned in 2009 in favor of work on
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML5' title='HTML5'>
[Text           ] HTML5
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] and
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/XHTML#XHTML5' title='XHTML'>
[Text           ] XHTML5
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] .
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-43' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-43'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 43
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-44' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-44'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 44
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-45' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-45'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 45
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[Text           ] XHTML 2.0 was incompatible with XHTML 1.x and, therefore, would be more accurately characterized as an XHTML-inspired new language than an update to XHTML 1.x.
[End Tag        ] </li>
[Start Tag      ] <li>
[Text           ] An XHTML syntax, known as "XHTML5.1", is being defined alongside
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML5' title='HTML5'>
[Text           ] HTML5
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] in the HTML5 draft.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-46' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-46'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 46
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </li>
[End Tag        ] </ul>
[Start Tag      ] <h2>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-headline' id='Markup'>
[Text           ] Markup
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection'>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection-bracket'>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=HTML&action=edit&section=6' title='Edit section: Markup'>
[Text           ] edit
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection-bracket'>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </h2>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] HTML markup consists of several key components, including
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] tags
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] (and their
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] attributes
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] ), character-based
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] data types
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] ,
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] character references
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] and
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] entity references
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] . Another important component is the
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Document_type_declaration' title='Document type declaration'>
[Text           ] document type declaration
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] , which triggers
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standards_mode' title='Standards mode' class='mw-redirect'>
[Text           ] standards mode
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] rendering.
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] The following is an example of the classic
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hello_world_program' title='Hello world program' class='mw-redirect'>
[Text           ] Hello world program
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] , a common test employed for comparing
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language' title='Programming language'>
[Text           ] programming languages
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] ,
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scripting_language' title='Scripting language'>
[Text           ] scripting languages
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] and
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Markup_language' title='Markup language'>
[Text           ] markup languages
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] . This example is made using 9
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lines_of_code' title='Lines of code' class='mw-redirect'>
[Text           ] lines of code
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] :
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <div dir='ltr' class='mw-geshi mw-code mw-content-ltr'>
[Start Tag      ] <div class='html5 source-html5'>
[Start Tag      ] <pre class='de1'>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc0'>
[Text           ] &lt;!DOCTYPE html&gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] html
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] head
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] title
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] This is a title
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] title
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] head
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] body
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] p
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] Hello world!
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] p
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] body
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] html
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </pre>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] (The text between &lt;html&gt; and &lt;/html&gt; describes the web page, and the text between &lt;body&gt; and &lt;/body&gt; is the visible page content. The markup text "&lt;title&gt;This is a title&lt;/title&gt;" defines the browser page title.)
[End Tag        ] </i>
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] The Document Type Declaration
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] &lt;!DOCTYPE html&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] is for HTML5. If a declaration is not included, various browsers will revert to "
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Quirks_mode' title='Quirks mode'>
[Text           ] quirks mode
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] " for rendering.
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-hsivonen_47-0' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-hsivonen-47'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 47
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <h3>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-headline' id='Elements'>
[Text           ] Elements
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection'>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection-bracket'>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=HTML&action=edit&section=7' title='Edit section: Elements'>
[Text           ] edit
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection-bracket'>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </h3>
[Start Tag      ] <div class='hatnote relarticle mainarticle'>
[Text           ] Main article:
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML_element' title='HTML element'>
[Text           ] HTML element
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] HTML documents imply a structure of nested
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML_element' title='HTML element'>
[Text           ] HTML elements
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] . These are indicated in the document by HTML
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] tags
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] , enclosed in angle brackets thus:
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;p&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Start Tag      ] <sup id='cite_ref-48' class='reference'>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTML?oldformat=true#cite_note-48'>
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] 48
[Start Tag      ] <span>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </a>
[End Tag        ] </sup>
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] In the simple, general case, the extent of an element is indicated by a pair of tags: a "start tag"
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;p&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] and "end tag"
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;/p&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] . The text content of the element, if any, is placed between these tags.
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] Tags may also enclose further tag markup between the start and end, including a mixture of tags and text. This indicates further, nested, elements, as children of the parent element.
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] The start tag may also include
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] attributes
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] within the tag. These indicate other information, such as identifiers for sections within the document, identifiers used to bind style information to the presentation of the document, and for some tags such as the
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;img&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] used to embed images, the reference to the image resource.
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] Some elements, such as the
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Line_breaking_character' title='Line breaking character' class='mw-redirect'>
[Text           ] line break
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;br&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] , do not permit
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] any
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] embedded content, either text or further tags. These require only a single empty tag (akin to a start tag) and do not use an end tag.
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] Many tags, particularly the closing end tag for the very commonly-used paragraph element
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;p&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] , are optional. An HTML browser or other agent can infer the closure for the end of an element from the context and the structural rules defined by the HTML standard. These rules are complex and not widely understood by most HTML coders.
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] The general form of an
[Start Tag      ] <b>
[Text           ] HTML element
[End Tag        ] </b>
[Text           ] is therefore:
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] &lt;tag attribute1="value1" attribute2="value2"&gt;
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] content
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] &lt;/tag&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] . Some HTML elements are defined as
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] empty elements
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] and take the form
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] &lt;tag attribute1="value1" attribute2="value2" &gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] . Empty elements may enclose no content, for instance, the BR tag or the inline IMG tag. The name of an HTML element is the name used in the tags. Note that the end tag's name is preceded by a slash character, "/", and that in empty elements the end tag is neither required nor allowed. If attributes are not mentioned, default values are used in each case.
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <h4>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-headline' id='Element_examples'>
[Text           ] Element examples
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection'>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection-bracket'>
[Text           ] [
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=HTML&action=edit&section=8' title='Edit section: Element examples'>
[Text           ] edit
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='mw-editsection-bracket'>
[Text           ] ]
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </h4>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] Header of the HTML document:&lt;head&gt;...&lt;/head&gt;. The title is included in the head, for example:
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <div dir='ltr' class='mw-geshi mw-code mw-content-ltr'>
[Start Tag      ] <div class='html4strict source-html4strict'>
[Start Tag      ] <pre class='de1'>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] head
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] title
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] The Title
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] title
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] head
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </pre>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] Headings: HTML headings are defined with the
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;h1&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] to
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;h6&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] tags:
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <div dir='ltr' class='mw-geshi mw-code mw-content-ltr'>
[Start Tag      ] <div class='html4strict source-html4strict'>
[Start Tag      ] <pre class='de1'>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] h1
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] Heading level 1
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] h1
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] h2
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] Heading level 2
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] h2
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] h3
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] Heading level 3
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] h3
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] h4
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] Heading level 4
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] h4
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] h5
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] Heading level 5
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] h5
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] h6
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] Heading level 6
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] h6
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </pre>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] Paragraphs:
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <div dir='ltr' class='mw-geshi mw-code mw-content-ltr'>
[Start Tag      ] <div class='html4strict source-html4strict'>
[Start Tag      ] <pre class='de1'>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] p
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] Paragraph 1
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] p
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] p
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] Paragraph 2
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] p
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </pre>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] Line breaks:
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;br&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] . The difference between
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;br&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] and
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;p&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] is that "br"
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Line_breaking_character' title='Line breaking character' class='mw-redirect'>
[Text           ] breaks a line
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] without altering the semantic structure of the page, whereas "p" sections the page into
[Start Tag      ] <a href='http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paragraph' title='Paragraph'>
[Text           ] paragraphs
[End Tag        ] </a>
[Text           ] . Note also that "br" is an
[Start Tag      ] <i>
[Text           ] empty element
[End Tag        ] </i>
[Text           ] in that, while it may have attributes, it can take no content and it may not have an end tag.
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <div dir='ltr' class='mw-geshi mw-code mw-content-ltr'>
[Start Tag      ] <div class='html4strict source-html4strict'>
[Start Tag      ] <pre class='de1'>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] p
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] This
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] br
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] is a paragraph
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] br
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] with
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] br
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] line breaks
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] p
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </pre>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] This is a link in HTML. To create a link the
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;a&gt;
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] tag is used. The
[Start Tag      ] <code>
[Text           ] href=
[End Tag        ] </code>
[Text           ] attribute holds the URL address of the link.
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <div dir='ltr' class='mw-geshi mw-code mw-content-ltr'>
[Start Tag      ] <div class='html4strict source-html4strict'>
[Start Tag      ] <pre class='de1'>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] a
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw3'>
[Text           ] href
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] =
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='st0'>
[Text           ] "http://www.google.com/"
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] A Link to Google!
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc2'>
[Text           ] &lt;
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sy0'>
[Text           ] /
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='kw2'>
[Text           ] a
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] &gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </pre>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Start Tag      ] <span id='Comments'>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Start Tag      ] <span id='comments'>
[End Tag        ] </span>
[Text           ] Comments:
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <div dir='ltr' class='mw-geshi mw-code mw-content-ltr'>
[Start Tag      ] <div class='html4strict source-html4strict'>
[Start Tag      ] <pre class='de1'>
[Start Tag      ] <span class='sc-1'>
[Text           ] &lt;!-- This is a comment --&gt;
[End Tag        ] </span>
[End Tag        ] </pre>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[End Tag        ] </div>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] Comments can help in the understanding of the markup and do not display in the webpage.
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <p>
[Text           ] There are several types of markup elements used in HTML:
[End Tag        ] </p>
[Start Tag      ] <dl>
[Start Tag      ] <dt>
[Text           ] Structural markup describes the purpose of text
[End Tag        ] </dt>
[Start Tag      ] <dd>
[Text           ] For example,
[Start Tag      ] <code class='nowrap' style>
[Text           ] &lt;h2&gt;Golf&lt;/h2&gt;
